the person who applied for the order under section  303Z41  agrees to its
payment, or

1.303Z44.7.b

the court has assessed the amount allowed in respect of that item and the sum
is paid in respect of the assessed amount.

1.303Z44.8

For the purposes of subsection  (7) —

1.303Z44.8.a

a “relevant item of expenditure” is an item of expenditure to which
regulations under section 286B would apply if the order under subsection  (1)
had instead been a recovery order;

1.303Z44.8.b

an amount is “allowed” in respect of a relevant item of expenditure if it
would have been allowed by those regulations.

1.303Z44.9

For the purposes of section 308(2), on the making of an order under subsection
(1) , the forfeitable property is to be treated as if it had been forfeited.

1.303Z44.10

If there is more than one item of associated property or more than one
excepted joint owner, the total amount to be paid under subsection  (1) , and
the part of that amount which is to be provided by each person who holds any
such associated property or who is an excepted joint owner, is to be agreed
between both (or all) of them and the person who applied for the order under
section  303Z41 .

1.303Z44.11

If the person who applied for the order under section  303Z41  was a
constable, an SFO officer or an accredited financial investigator, that person
may enter into an agreement for the purposes of any provision of this section
only if the person is a senior officer or is authorised to do so by a senior
officer.

1.303Z44.12

An amount received under an order under subsection  (1)  must be applied as
follows—

1.303Z44.12.a

first, it must be applied in making any payment of legal expenses which, after
giving effect to subsection  (7) , are payable under this subsection in
pursuance of provision under subsection  (6) ;

1.303Z44.12.b

second, it must be applied in payment or reimbursement of any reasonable costs
incurred in storing or insuring the forfeitable property and any associated
property whilst detained under this Part;

1.303Z44.12.c

third, it must be paid—

1.303Z44.12.c.i

if the order was made by a magistrates’ court, into the Consolidated Fund;

1.303Z44.12.c.ii

if the order was made by the sheriff, into the Scottish Consolidated Fund.

########### Associated and joint property: default of agreement

1.303Z45

1.303Z45.1

Where this section applies and there is no agreement under section  303Z44 ,
the magistrates’ court or sheriff may transfer the application made under
section  303Z41  to the appropriate court.

1.303Z45.2

The “appropriate court” is—

1.303Z45.2.a

the High Court, where the application under section  303Z41  was made to a
magistrates’ court;

1.303Z45.2.b

the Court of Session, where the application under section  303Z41  was made to
the sheriff.

1.303Z45.3

Where (under subsection  (1) ) an application made under section  303Z41  is
transferred to the appropriate court, the appropriate court may order the
forfeiture of the property to which the application relates, or any part of
that property, if satisfied that what is to be forfeited is recoverable
property or intended by any person for use in unlawful conduct.

1.303Z45.4

An order under subsection  (3)  made by the High Court may include provision
of the type that may be included in an order under section  303Z41 (4)  made
by a magistrates’ court by virtue of section  303Z41 (5) .

1.303Z45.5

If provision is included in an order of the High Court by virtue of subsection
(4)  of this section, section  303Z41 (6)  and  (7)  apply with the necessary
modifications.

1.303Z45.6

The appropriate court may, as well as making an order under subsection  (3) ,
make an order—

1.303Z45.6.a

providing for the forfeiture of the associated property or (as the case may
be) for the excepted joint owner‘s interest to be extinguished, or

1.303Z45.6.b

providing for the excepted joint owner‘s interest to be severed.

1.303Z45.7

Where (under subsection  (1) ) the magistrates’ court or sheriff decides not
to transfer an application made under section  303Z41  to the appropriate
court, the magistrates’ court or sheriff may, as well as making an order under
section  303Z41 (4) , make an order—

1.303Z45.7.a

providing for the forfeiture of the associated property or (as the case may
be) for the excepted joint owner‘s interest to be extinguished, or

1.303Z45.7.b

providing for the excepted joint owner‘s interest to be severed.

1.303Z45.8

An order under subsection  (6)  or  (7)  may be made only if the appropriate
court, the magistrates’ court or the sheriff (as the case may be) thinks it
just and equitable to do so.

1.303Z45.9

An order under subsection  (6)  or  (7)  must provide for the payment of an
amount to the person who holds the associated property or who is an excepted
joint owner.

1.303Z45.10

In making an order under subsection  (6)  or  (7) , and including provision in
it by virtue of subsection  (9) , the appropriate court, the magistrates’
court or the sheriff (as the case may be) must have regard to—

1.303Z45.10.a

the rights of any person who holds the associated property or who is an
excepted joint owner and the value to that person of that property or (as the
case may be) of that person‘s share (including any value that cannot be
assessed in terms of money), and

1.303Z45.10.b

the interest of the person who applied for the order under section  303Z41  in
realising the value of the forfeitable property.

1.303Z45.11

If the appropriate court, the magistrates’ court or the sheriff (as the case
may be) is satisfied that—

1.303Z45.11.a

the person who holds the associated property or who is an excepted joint owner
has suffered loss as a result of—

1.303Z45.11.a.i

the seizure of the forfeitable property under section  303Z29  and its
subsequent detention, or

1.303Z45.11.a.ii

the making of the crypto wallet freezing order under section  303Z37 , and

1.303Z45.11.b

the circumstances are exceptional,

an order under subsection  (6)  or  (7)  may require the payment of
compensation to that person.

1.303Z45.12

The amount of compensation to be paid by virtue of subsection  (11)  is the
amount the appropriate court, the magistrates’ court or the sheriff (as the
case may be) thinks reasonable, having regard to the loss suffered and any
other relevant circumstances.

1.303Z45.13

Compensation to be paid by virtue of subsection  (11)  is to be paid in the
same way that compensation is to be paid under section  303Z52 .

########### Continuation of crypto wallet freezing order pending appeal

1.303Z46

1.303Z46.1

This section applies where, on an application under section  303Z41  in
relation to a crypto wallet to which a crypto wallet freezing order applies—

1.303Z46.1.a

the magistrates’ court or sheriff decides—

1.303Z46.1.a.i

to make an order under section 303Z41(4) in relation to some but not all of
the cryptoassets to which the application related, or

1.303Z46.1.a.ii

not to make an order under section 303Z41(4), or

1.303Z46.1.b

if the application is transferred in accordance with section 303Z45(1), the
High Court or Court of Session decides—

1.303Z46.1.b.i

to make an order under section 303Z45(3) in relation to some but not all of
the cryptoassets to which the application related, or

1.303Z46.1.b.ii

not to make an order under section 303Z45(3).

1.303Z46.2

The person who made the application under section  303Z41  may apply without
notice to the court or sheriff that made the decision referred to in
subsection (1) for an order that the crypto wallet freezing order is to
continue to have effect.

1.303Z46.3

Where the court or sheriff makes an order under subsection  (2)  the crypto
wallet freezing order is to continue to have effect until—

1.303Z46.3.a

the end of the period of 48 hours starting with the making of the order under
subsection  (2) , or

1.303Z46.3.b

if within that period of 48 hours an appeal is brought (whether under section
303Z47  or otherwise) against the decision referred to in subsection (1), the
time when the appeal is determined or otherwise disposed of.

1.303Z46.4

Subsection  (3)  of section  303Z31  applies for the purposes of subsection
(3)  as it applies for the purposes of that section.

########### Sections 

1.303Z47

1.303Z47.1

Any party to proceedings for an order for the forfeiture of cryptoassets under
section  303Z41  may appeal against—

1.303Z47.1.a

the making of an order under section  303Z41 ;

1.303Z47.1.b

the making of an order under section  303Z45 (7) ;

1.303Z47.1.c

a decision not to make an order under section  303Z41  unless the reason that
no order was made is that an order was instead made under section  303Z44 ;

1.303Z47.1.d

a decision not to make an order under section  303Z45 (7) .

Paragraphs  (c)  and  (d)  do not apply if the application for the order under
section  303Z41  was transferred in accordance with section  303Z45 (1) .

1.303Z47.2

Where an order under section  303Z44  is made by a magistrates’ court, any
party to the proceedings for the order (including any party to the proceedings
under section  303Z41  that preceded the making of the order) may appeal
against a decision to include, or not to include, provision in the order under
section  303Z44 (6) .

1.303Z47.3

An appeal under this section lies—

1.303Z47.3.a

in relation to England and Wales, to the Crown Court;

1.303Z47.3.b

in relation to Scotland, to the Sheriff Appeal Court;

1.303Z47.3.c

in relation to Northern Ireland, to a county court.

1.303Z47.4

An appeal under this section must be made before the end of the period of 30
days starting with the day on which the court or sheriff makes the order or
decision.

1.303Z47.5

The court hearing the appeal may make any order it thinks appropriate.

1.303Z47.6

If the court upholds an appeal against an order forfeiting any cryptoasset or
other item of property, it may order the release of the whole or any part of
the property.

########### Realisation or destruction of forfeited cryptoassets etc

1.303Z48

1.303Z48.1

This section applies where any cryptoasset or other item of property is
forfeited under this Chapter.

1.303Z48.2

An enforcement officer must—

1.303Z48.2.a

realise the property, or

1.303Z48.2.b

make arrangements for its realisation.

This is subject to subsections  (3)  to  (5) .

1.303Z48.3

The property is not to be realised—

1.303Z48.3.a

before the end of the period within which an appeal may be made (whether under
section  303Z47  or otherwise), or

1.303Z48.3.b

if an appeal is made within that period, before the appeal is determined or
otherwise disposed of.

1.303Z48.4

The realisation of property under subsection  (2)  must be carried out, so far
as practicable, in the manner best calculated to maximise the amount obtained
for the property.

1.303Z48.5

Where an enforcement officer is satisfied that—

1.303Z48.5.a

it is not reasonably practicable to realise any cryptoasset, or

1.303Z48.5.b

there are reasonable grounds to believe that the realisation of any
cryptoasset would be contrary to the public interest,

the enforcement officer may destroy the cryptoasset.

1.303Z48.6

But—

1.303Z48.6.a

the enforcement officer may destroy the cryptoasset only if the officer is a
senior officer or is authorised to do so by a senior officer, and

1.303Z48.6.b

the cryptoasset is not to be destroyed—

1.303Z48.6.b.i

before the end of the period within which an appeal may be made (whether under
section  303Z47  or otherwise), or

1.303Z48.6.b.ii

if an appeal is made within that period, before the appeal is determined or
otherwise disposed of.

1.303Z48.7

The question of whether the realisation of the cryptoasset would be contrary
to the public interest is to be determined with particular reference to how
likely it is that the entry of the cryptoasset into general circulation would
facilitate criminal conduct by any person.

########### Proceeds of realisation

1.303Z49

1.303Z49.1

This section applies where any cryptoasset or other item of property is
realised under section  303Z48 .

1.303Z49.2

The proceeds of the realisation must be applied as follows—

1.303Z49.2.a

first, they must be applied in making any payment required to be made by
virtue of section  303Z45 (9) ;

1.303Z49.2.b

second, they must be applied in making any payment of legal expenses which,
after giving effect to section  303Z41 (6)  (including as applied by section
303Z45 (5) ), are payable under this subsection in pursuance of provision
under section  303Z41 (5)  or, as the case may be,  303Z45 (4) ;

1.303Z49.2.c

third, they must be applied in payment or reimbursement of any reasonable
costs incurred in storing or insuring the property whilst detained under this
Part and in realising the property;

1.303Z49.2.d

fourth, they must be paid—

1.303Z49.2.d.i

if the property was forfeited by a magistrates’ court or the High Court, into
the Consolidated Fund;

1.303Z49.2.d.ii

if the property was forfeited by the sheriff or the Court of Session, into the
Scottish Consolidated Fund.

1.303Z49.3

If what is realised under section  303Z48  represents part only of an item of
property, the reference in subsection  (2)(c)  to costs incurred in storing or
insuring the property is to be read as a reference to costs incurred in
storing or insuring the whole of the property.

########## Supplementary

########### Victims and other owners: detained cryptoassets

1.303Z50

1.303Z50.1

A person who claims that any cryptoassets detained under this Part belong to
the person may apply for some or all of the cryptoassets to be released.

1.303Z50.2

An application under subsection  (1)  is to be made—

1.303Z50.2.a

in England and Wales or Northern Ireland, to a magistrates’ court;

1.303Z50.2.b

in Scotland, to the sheriff.

1.303Z50.3

The application may be made in the course of proceedings under section  303Z32
or  303Z41  or at any other time.

1.303Z50.4

The court or sheriff may order the cryptoassets to which the application
relates to be released to the applicant if it appears to the court or sheriff
that—

1.303Z50.4.a

the applicant was deprived of the cryptoassets to which the application
relates, or of property which they represent, by unlawful conduct,

1.303Z50.4.b

the cryptoassets the applicant was deprived of were not, immediately before
the applicant was deprived of them, recoverable property, and

1.303Z50.4.c

the cryptoassets belong to the applicant.

1.303Z50.5

If subsection  (6)  applies, the court or sheriff may order the cryptoassets
to which the application relates to be released to the applicant or to the
person from whom they were seized.

1.303Z50.6

This subsection applies where—

1.303Z50.6.a

the applicant is not the person from whom the cryptoassets to which the
application relates were seized,

1.303Z50.6.b

it appears to the court or sheriff that those cryptoassets belong to the
applicant,

1.303Z50.6.c

the court or sheriff is satisfied that the release condition is met in
relation to those cryptoassets, and

1.303Z50.6.d

no objection to the making of an order under subsection  (5)  has been made by
the person from whom those cryptoassets were seized.

1.303Z50.7

The release condition is met—

1.303Z50.7.a

if the conditions in Chapter 3C for the detention of the cryptoassets are no
longer met, or

1.303Z50.7.b

in relation to cryptoassets which are subject to an application for forfeiture
under section  303Z41 , if the court or sheriff decides not to make an order
under that section in relation to the cryptoassets.

########### Victims and other owners: crypto wallet freezing orders

1.303Z51

1.303Z51.1

A person who claims that any cryptoassets held in a crypto wallet in respect
of which a crypto wallet freezing order has effect belong to the person may
apply for some or all of the cryptoassets to be released.

1.303Z51.2

An application under subsection  (1)  is to be made—

1.303Z51.2.a

in England and Wales or Northern Ireland, to a magistrates’ court;

1.303Z51.2.b

in Scotland, to the sheriff.

1.303Z51.3

The application may be made in the course of proceedings under section  303Z37
or  303Z41  or at any other time.

1.303Z51.4

The court or sheriff may, subject to subsection (8), order the cryptoassets to
which the application relates to be released to the applicant if it appears to
the court or sheriff that—

1.303Z51.4.a

the applicant was deprived of the cryptoassets to which the application
relates, or of property which they represent, by unlawful conduct,

1.303Z51.4.b

the cryptoassets the applicant was deprived of were not, immediately before
the applicant was deprived of them, recoverable property, and

1.303Z51.4.c

the cryptoassets belong to the applicant.

1.303Z51.5

If subsection  (6)  applies, the court or sheriff may, subject to subsection
(8), order the cryptoassets to which the application relates to be released to
the applicant.

1.303Z51.6

This subsection applies where—

1.303Z51.6.a

the applicant is not the person from whom the cryptoassets to which the
application relates were seized,

1.303Z51.6.b

it appears to the court or sheriff that those cryptoassets belong to the
applicant,

1.303Z51.6.c

the court or sheriff is satisfied that the release condition is met in
relation to those cryptoassets, and

1.303Z51.6.d

no objection to the making of an order under subsection  (5)  has been made by
the person from whom those cryptoassets were seized.

1.303Z51.7

The release condition is met—

1.303Z51.7.a

if the conditions for the making of the crypto wallet freezing order are no
longer met in relation to the cryptoassets to which the application relates,
or

1.303Z51.7.b

in relation to cryptoassets held in a crypto wallet subject to a crypto wallet
freezing order which are subject to an application for forfeiture under
section  303Z41 , if the court or sheriff decides not to make an order under
that section in relation to the cryptoassets.

1.303Z51.8

If an application under section 303Z41 is made for the forfeiture of the
cryptoassets, the cryptoassets are not to be released under this section until
any proceedings in pursuance of the application (including any proceedings on
appeal) are concluded.

1.303Z51.9

In relation to cryptoassets held in a crypto wallet that is subject to a
crypto wallet freezing order, references in this section to a person from whom
cryptoassets were seized include a reference to a person by or for whom the
crypto wallet was administered immediately before the crypto wallet freezing
order was made.

########### Compensation

1.303Z52

1.303Z52.1

This section applies if no order is made under section  303Z41 ,  303Z44  or
303Z45  in respect of cryptoassets detained under this Part or held in a
crypto wallet that is subject to a crypto wallet freezing order under section
303Z37 .

1.303Z52.2

Where this section applies, the following may make an application to the
relevant court for compensation—

1.303Z52.2.a

a person to whom the cryptoassets belong or from whom they were seized, or

1.303Z52.2.b

a person by or for whom a crypto wallet to which the crypto wallet freezing
order applies is administered.

1.303Z52.3

If the relevant court is satisfied that the applicant has suffered loss as a
result of the detention of the cryptoassets or the making of the crypto wallet
freezing order and that the circumstances are exceptional, the relevant court
may order compensation to be paid to the applicant.

1.303Z52.4

The amount of compensation to be paid is the amount the relevant court thinks
reasonable, having regard to the loss suffered and any other relevant
circumstances.

1.303Z52.5

If the cryptoassets were seized, or the crypto wallet freezing order was
applied for, by an officer of Revenue and Customs, the compensation is to be
paid by the Commissioners for His Majesty’s Revenue and Customs.

1.303Z52.6

If the cryptoassets were seized, or the crypto wallet freezing order was
applied for, by a constable, the compensation is to be paid as follows—

1.303Z52.6.a

in the case of a constable of a police force in England and Wales, it is to be
paid out of the police fund from which the expenses of the police force are
met;

1.303Z52.6.b

in the case of a constable of the Police Service of Scotland, it is to be paid
by the Scottish Police Authority;

1.303Z52.6.c

in the case of a police officer within the meaning of the Police (Northern
Ireland) Act 2000, it is to be paid out of money provided by the Chief
Constable of the Police Service of Northern Ireland.

1.303Z52.7

If the cryptoassets were seized, or the crypto wallet freezing order was
applied for, by an SFO officer, the compensation is to be paid by the Director
of the Serious Fraud Office.

1.303Z52.8

If the cryptoassets were seized, or the crypto wallet freezing order was
applied for, by a National Crime Agency officer, the compensation is to be
paid by the National Crime Agency.

1.303Z52.9

If the cryptoassets were seized, or the crypto wallet freezing order was
applied for, by an accredited financial investigator who was not an officer of
Revenue and Customs, a constable, an SFO officer or a National Crime Agency
officer, the compensation is to be paid as follows—

1.303Z52.9.a

in the case of an investigator who was—

1.303Z52.9.a.i

a member of the civilian staff of a police force (including the metropolitan
police force), within the meaning of Part 1 of the Police Reform and Social
Responsibility Act 2011, or

1.303Z52.9.a.ii

a member of staff of the City of London police force,

it is to be paid out of the police fund from which the expenses of the police
force are met,

1.303Z52.9.b

in the case of an investigator who was a member of staff of the Police Service
of Northern Ireland, it is to be paid out of money provided by the Chief
Constable of the Police Service of Northern Ireland,

1.303Z52.9.c

in the case of an investigator who was a member of staff of a department of
the Government of the United Kingdom, it is to be paid by the Minister of the
Crown in charge of the department or by the department,

1.303Z52.9.d

in the case of an investigator who was a member of staff of a Northern Ireland
department, it is to be paid by the department,

1.303Z52.9.e

in the case of an investigator who was exercising a function of the Welsh
Revenue Authority, it is to be paid by the Welsh Revenue Authority, and

1.303Z52.9.f

in any other case, it is to be paid by the employer of the investigator.

1.303Z52.10

The Secretary of State may by regulations amend subsection  (9) .

1.303Z52.11

The power in subsection  (10)  is exercisable by the Department of Justice
(and not by the Secretary of State) so far as it may be used to make provision
that—

1.303Z52.11.a

would be within the legislative competence of the Northern Ireland Assembly if
contained in an Act of that Assembly, and

1.303Z52.11.b

would not, if contained in a Bill for an Act of the Northern Ireland Assembly,
result in the Bill requiring the consent of the Secretary of State.

1.303Z52.12

If an order under section  303Z37 ,  303Z41 ,  303Z44  or  303Z45  is made in
respect of some of the cryptoassets detained or held, this section has effect
in relation to the remainder.

1.303Z52.13

In this section “ relevant court ” means—

1.303Z52.13.a

in England and Wales and Northern Ireland, a magistrates’ court, and

1.303Z52.13.b

in Scotland, the sheriff.

########### Powers for prosecutors to appear in proceedings

1.303Z53

1.303Z53.1

The Director of Public Prosecutions or the Director of Public Prosecutions for
Northern Ireland may appear for a constable or an accredited financial
investigator in proceedings under this Chapter if the Director—

1.303Z53.1.a

is asked by, or on behalf of, a constable or (as the case may be) an
accredited financial investigator to do so, and

1.303Z53.1.b

considers it appropriate to do so.

1.303Z53.2

The Director of Public Prosecutions may appear for the Commissioners for His
Majesty’s Revenue and Customs or an officer of Revenue and Customs in
proceedings under this Chapter if the Director—

1.303Z53.2.a

is asked by, or on behalf of, the Commissioners for His Majesty’s Revenue and
Customs or (as the case may be) an officer of Revenue and Customs to do so,
and

1.303Z53.2.b

considers it appropriate to do so.

1.303Z53.3

The Directors may charge fees for the provision of services under this
section.

1.303Z53.4

The references in subsection  (1)  to an accredited financial investigator do
not include an accredited financial investigator who is an officer of Revenue
and Customs but the references in subsection  (2)  to an officer of Revenue
and Customs do include an accredited financial investigator who is an officer
of Revenue and Customs.

######### Conversion of cryptoassets

########## Conversion

########### Detained cryptoassets: conversion

1.303Z54

1.303Z54.1

Subsection  (2)  applies while any cryptoassets are detained in pursuance of
an order under section  303Z30  or  303Z32  (including where cryptoassets are
subject to forfeiture proceedings).

1.303Z54.2

A person within subsection  (3)  may apply to the relevant court for an order
requiring all of the cryptoassets detained pursuant to the order to be
converted into money.

1.303Z54.3

The following persons are within this subsection—

1.303Z54.3.a

an enforcement officer;

1.303Z54.3.b

a person from whom the cryptoassets were seized.

1.303Z54.4

In deciding whether to make an order under this section, the court must have
regard to whether the cryptoassets (as a whole) are likely to suffer a
significant loss in value during the period before they are released or
forfeited (including the period during which an appeal against an order for
forfeiture may be made).

1.303Z54.5

Before making an order under this section the court must give an opportunity
to be heard to—

1.303Z54.5.a

the parties to the proceedings, and

1.303Z54.5.b

any other person who may be affected by its decision.

1.303Z54.6

As soon as practicable after an order is made under this section, an
enforcement officer must convert the cryptoassets, or arrange for the
cryptoassets to be converted, into money.

1.303Z54.7

The conversion of cryptoassets under subsection  (6)  must be carried out, so
far as practicable, in the manner best calculated to maximise the amount of
money obtained for the cryptoassets.

1.303Z54.8

At the first opportunity after the cryptoassets are converted, the enforcement
officer must arrange for the amount of money obtained for the cryptoassets to
be paid into an interest-bearing account and held there.

1.303Z54.9

Interest accruing on the amount is to be added to it on its forfeiture or
release.

1.303Z54.10

Where cryptoassets are converted into money in accordance with an order made
under this section—

1.303Z54.10.a

the cryptoassets are no longer to be treated as being detained in pursuance of
an order under section  303Z30  or  303Z32 , and

1.303Z54.10.b

any application made under section  303Z41 (2)  in relation to the
cryptoassets which has not yet been determined or otherwise disposed of
(including under section  303Z44  or  303Z45 ) is to be treated as if it were
an application made under section  303Z60 (2)  in relation to the converted
cryptoassets.

1.303Z54.11

An order made under this section must provide for notice to be given to
persons affected by the order.

1.303Z54.12

No appeal may be made against an order made under this section.

########### Frozen crypto wallet: conversion

1.303Z55

1.303Z55.1

This section applies while a crypto wallet freezing order under section
303Z37  has effect (including where cryptoassets held in a crypto wallet that
is subject to a crypto wallet freezing order are subject to forfeiture
proceedings).

1.303Z55.2

A person within subsection  (3)  may apply to the relevant court for an order
requiring all of the cryptoassets held in the crypto wallet to be converted
into money.

1.303Z55.3

The following persons are within this subsection—

1.303Z55.3.a

an enforcement officer;

1.303Z55.3.b

a person by or for whom the crypto wallet is administered.

1.303Z55.4

In deciding whether to make an order under this section, the court must have
regard to whether the cryptoassets (as a whole) are likely to suffer a
significant loss in value during the period before—

1.303Z55.4.a

the crypto wallet freezing order ceases to have effect, or

1.303Z55.4.b

the cryptoassets are forfeited (including the period during which an appeal
against an order for forfeiture may be made).

1.303Z55.5

Before making an order under this section the court must give an opportunity
to be heard to—

1.303Z55.5.a

the parties to the proceedings, and

1.303Z55.5.b

any other person who may be affected by its decision.

1.303Z55.6

As soon as practicable after an order is made under this section, the UK-
connected cryptoasset service provider that administers the crypto wallet must
convert the cryptoassets, or arrange for the cryptoassets to be converted,
into money.

1.303Z55.7

The conversion of cryptoassets under subsection  (6)  must be carried out, so
far as practicable, in the manner best calculated to maximise the amount of
money obtained for the cryptoassets.

1.303Z55.8

At the first opportunity after the cryptoassets are converted, the UK-
connected cryptoasset service provider must arrange for the amount of money
obtained for the cryptoassets to be paid into an interest-bearing account
nominated by an enforcement officer and held there.

1.303Z55.9

But—

1.303Z55.9.a

the UK-connected cryptoasset service provider may deduct any reasonable
expenses incurred by the provider in connection with the conversion of the
cryptoassets, and

1.303Z55.9.b

the amount to be treated as the proceeds of the conversion of the cryptoassets
is to be reduced accordingly.

1.303Z55.10

Interest accruing on the amount obtained for the cryptoassets is to be added
to it on its forfeiture or release.

1.303Z55.11

Where cryptoassets are converted in accordance with an order made under this
section—

1.303Z55.11.a

the crypto wallet freezing order ceases to have effect,

1.303Z55.11.b

any application made under section  303Z41 (2)  in relation to the
cryptoassets which has not yet been determined or otherwise disposed of
(including under section  303Z44  or  303Z45 ) is to be treated as if it were
an application made under section  303Z60 (2)  in relation to the converted
cryptoassets, and

1.303Z55.11.c

any application made under section  303Z46 (2)  in relation to the crypto
wallet which has not yet been determined or otherwise disposed of may not be
proceeded with.

1.303Z55.12

An order made under this section must provide for notice to be given to
persons affected by the order.

1.303Z55.13

No appeal may be made against an order made under this section.

########### Conversion: existing forfeiture proceedings

1.303Z56

1.303Z56.1

Where—

1.303Z56.1.a

cryptoassets are forfeited under section  303Z41  or  303Z45 , and

1.303Z56.1.b

before the cryptoassets are realised or destroyed in accordance with section
303Z48 , an order is made under section  303Z54  requiring the cryptoassets to
be converted into money,

section  303Z62 (1)  applies in relation to the converted cryptoassets as if
they had been detained under section  303Z57  and forfeited under section
303Z60  (and accordingly section  303Z48  ceases to apply).

1.303Z56.2

Where—

1.303Z56.2.a

cryptoassets are forfeited under section  303Z41  or  303Z45 , and

1.303Z56.2.b

before the cryptoassets are realised or destroyed in accordance with section
303Z48 , an order is made under section  303Z55  requiring the cryptoassets to
be converted into money,

section  303Z62 (2)  applies in relation to the converted cryptoassets as if
they had been detained under section  303Z58  and forfeited under section
303Z60  (and accordingly section  303Z48  ceases to apply).

1.303Z56.3

Where—

1.303Z56.3.a

an appeal may be made under section  303Z47 (1)  or  (2)  in relation to the
determination of an application under section  303Z41 (2)  for the forfeiture
of cryptoassets (including where section  303Z44  or  303Z45  applies), and

1.303Z56.3.b

an order is made under section  303Z54  or  303Z55  requiring the cryptoassets
to be converted into money,

the appeal may instead be made under section  303Z61  (within the time allowed
by section  303Z47 (4) ) as if it were an appeal against the determination of
an application under section  303Z60 .

1.303Z56.4

Where—

1.303Z56.4.a

an appeal is made under section  303Z47 (1)  or  (2)  in relation to the
determination of an application under section  303Z41 (2)  for the forfeiture
of cryptoassets (including where section  303Z44  or  303Z45  applies), and

1.303Z56.4.b

before the appeal is determined or otherwise disposed of, an order is made
under section  303Z54  or  303Z55  requiring the cryptoassets to be converted
into money,

the appeal is to be treated as if it had been made under section  303Z61 (1)
in relation to the determination of an application under section  303Z60  for
the forfeiture of the converted cryptoassets.

########## Detention

########### Detained cryptoassets: detention of proceeds of conversion

1.303Z57

1.303Z57.1

This section applies where cryptoassets are converted into money in accordance
with an order under section  303Z54 .

1.303Z57.2

The proceeds of the conversion (the “converted cryptoassets”) may be detained
initially until the end of the period that the cryptoassets could, immediately
before the conversion, have been detained under Chapter 3C (ignoring the
possibility of any extension of that period).

1.303Z57.3

The period for which the converted cryptoassets may be detained may be
extended by an order made by the relevant court.

1.303Z57.4

An order under subsection  (3)  may not authorise the detention of the
converted cryptoassets beyond the end of the period of 2 years beginning with
the relevant date; but this is subject to subsection  (5) .

1.303Z57.5

The relevant court may make an order for the period of 2 years in subsection
(4)  to be extended to a period of up to 3 years beginning with the relevant
date.

1.303Z57.6

In subsections  (4)  and  (5)  “ the relevant date ” means the date on which
the first order under section  303Z30  or  303Z32  (as the case may be) was
made in relation to the cryptoassets.

1.303Z57.7

An application for an order under subsection  (3)  or  (5)  may be made—

1.303Z57.7.a

in relation to England and Wales and Northern Ireland, by—

1.303Z57.7.a.i

the Commissioners for His Majesty’s Revenue and Customs,

1.303Z57.7.a.ii

a constable,

1.303Z57.7.a.iii

an SFO officer, or

1.303Z57.7.a.iv

an accredited financial investigator who falls within a description specified
in an order made for the purposes of this Chapter by the Secretary of State or
the Welsh Ministers under section 453, and

1.303Z57.7.b

in relation to Scotland, by the Scottish Ministers in connection with their
functions under section  303Z41  or by a procurator fiscal.

1.303Z57.8

The relevant court may make an order under subsection  (3)  only if satisfied
that there are reasonable grounds for suspecting that the converted
cryptoassets to be further detained—

1.303Z57.8.a

are recoverable property, or

1.303Z57.8.b

are intended by any person for use in unlawful conduct.

1.303Z57.9

The relevant court may make an order under subsection  (5)  only if satisfied
that a request for assistance is outstanding in relation to the cryptoassets
mentioned in subsection  (1) .

1.303Z57.10

A “request for assistance” in subsection  (9)  means a request for assistance
in obtaining evidence (including information in any form or article) in
connection with the cryptoassets, made—

1.303Z57.10.a

by a judicial authority in the United Kingdom under section 7 of the Crime
(International Co-operation) Act 2003,

1.303Z57.10.b

by an enforcement officer, to an authority exercising equivalent functions in
a foreign country,

1.303Z57.10.c

by the Scottish Ministers in connection with their functions under this Part,
to an authority exercising equivalent functions in a foreign country, or

1.303Z57.10.d

by a person under section 375A or 408A (evidence overseas).

########### Frozen crypto wallets: detention of proceeds of conversion

1.303Z58

1.303Z58.1

This section applies where cryptoassets held in a crypto wallet subject to a
crypto wallet freezing order are converted into money in accordance with an
order under section  303Z55 .

1.303Z58.2

The proceeds of the conversion (the “converted cryptoassets”) may be detained
initially until the end of the period that the crypto wallet freezing order
was, immediately before the conversion, due to have effect under Chapter 3D
(ignoring the possibility of any extension of that period).

1.303Z58.3

The period for which the converted cryptoassets may be detained may be
extended by an order made by the relevant court.

1.303Z58.4

An order under subsection  (3)  may not authorise the detention of the
converted cryptoassets beyond the end of the period of 2 years beginning with
the day on which the crypto wallet freezing order was made; but this is
subject to subsection  (5) .

1.303Z58.5

The relevant court may make an order for the period of 2 years in subsection
(4)  to be extended to a period of up to 3 years beginning with the day on
which the crypto wallet freezing order was made.

1.303Z58.6

An application for an order under subsection  (3)  or  (5)  may be made—

1.303Z58.6.a

in relation to England and Wales and Northern Ireland, by—

1.303Z58.6.a.i

the Commissioners for His Majesty’s Revenue and Customs,

1.303Z58.6.a.ii

a constable,

1.303Z58.6.a.iii

an SFO officer, or

1.303Z58.6.a.iv

an accredited financial investigator who falls within a description specified
in an order made for the purposes of this Chapter by the Secretary of State or
the Welsh Ministers under section 453, and

1.303Z58.6.b

in relation to Scotland, by the Scottish Ministers in connection with their
functions under section  303Z41  or by a procurator fiscal.

1.303Z58.7

The relevant court may make an order under subsection  (3)  only if satisfied
that there are reasonable grounds for suspecting that the converted
cryptoassets to be further detained—

1.303Z58.7.a

are recoverable property, or

1.303Z58.7.b

are intended by any person for use in unlawful conduct.

1.303Z58.8

The relevant court may make an order under subsection  (5)  only if satisfied
that a request for assistance is outstanding in relation to the cryptoassets
mentioned in subsection  (1) .

1.303Z58.9

A “request for assistance” in subsection  (8)  means a request for assistance
in obtaining evidence (including information in any form or article) in
connection with the cryptoassets, made—

1.303Z58.9.a

by a judicial authority in the United Kingdom under section 7 of the Crime
(International Co-operation) Act 2003,

1.303Z58.9.b

by an enforcement officer, to an authority exercising equivalent functions in
a foreign country,

1.303Z58.9.c

by the Scottish Ministers in connection with their functions under this Part,
to an authority exercising equivalent functions in a foreign country, or

1.303Z58.9.d

by a person under section 375A or 408A (evidence overseas).

########## Release

########### Release of detained converted cryptoassets

1.303Z59

1.303Z59.1

This section applies while any converted cryptoassets are detained under
section  303Z57  or  303Z58 .

1.303Z59.2

The relevant court may direct the release of the whole or any part of the
converted cryptoassets if the following condition is met.

1.303Z59.3

The condition is that, on an application by the relevant person, the court is
not satisfied that there are reasonable grounds for suspecting that the
converted cryptoassets to be released—

1.303Z59.3.a

are recoverable property, or

1.303Z59.3.b

are intended by any person for use in unlawful conduct.

1.303Z59.4

In subsection  (3)  “ the relevant person ” means—

1.303Z59.4.a

in the case of converted cryptoassets detained under section  303Z57 , the
person from whom the cryptoassets mentioned in subsection  (1)  of that
section were seized, and

1.303Z59.4.b

in the case of converted cryptoassets detained under section  303Z58 , any
person affected by the crypto wallet freezing order mentioned in subsection
(1)  of that section.

1.303Z59.5

A person within subsection  (6)  may, after notifying the magistrates’ court
or sheriff under whose order converted cryptoassets are being detained,
release the whole or any part of the converted cryptoassets if satisfied that
the detention is no longer justified.

1.303Z59.6

The following persons are within this subsection—

1.303Z59.6.a

in relation to England and Wales or Northern Ireland, an enforcement officer;

1.303Z59.6.b

in relation to Scotland—

1.303Z59.6.b.i

the Scottish Ministers,

1.303Z59.6.b.ii

an officer of Revenue and Customs,

1.303Z59.6.b.iii

a constable, and

1.303Z59.6.b.iv

a procurator fiscal.

########## Forfeiture

########### Forfeiture order

1.303Z60

1.303Z60.1

This section applies while any converted cryptoassets are detained under
section  303Z57  or  303Z58 .

1.303Z60.2

An application for the forfeiture of some or all of the converted cryptoassets
may be made—

1.303Z60.2.a

to a magistrates’ court by a person within subsection  (3) , or

1.303Z60.2.b

to the sheriff by the Scottish Ministers.

1.303Z60.3

The following persons are within this subsection—

1.303Z60.3.a

the Commissioners for His Majesty’s Revenue and Customs,

1.303Z60.3.b

a constable,

1.303Z60.3.c

an SFO officer, and

1.303Z60.3.d

an accredited financial investigator who falls within a description specified
in an order made for the purposes of this Chapter by the Secretary of State or
the Welsh Ministers under section 453.

1.303Z60.4

The court or sheriff may order the forfeiture of some or all of the converted
cryptoassets if satisfied that the converted cryptoassets to be forfeited—

1.303Z60.4.a

are recoverable property, or

1.303Z60.4.b

are intended by any person for use in unlawful conduct.

1.303Z60.5

But in the case of recoverable property which belongs to joint tenants, one of
whom is an excepted joint owner, the order may not apply to so much of it as
the court thinks is attributable to the excepted joint owner’s share.

1.303Z60.6

Where an application for forfeiture is made under this section, the converted
cryptoassets are to continue to be detained under section  303Z57  or  303Z58
(and may not be released under any power conferred by this Chapter) until any
proceedings in pursuance of the application (including any proceedings on
appeal) are concluded.

########### Appeal against decision under section 

1.303Z61

1.303Z61.1

Any party to proceedings for an order for the forfeiture of converted
cryptoassets under section  303Z60  who is aggrieved by an order under that
section or by the decision of the court not to make such an order may appeal—

1.303Z61.1.a

from an order or decision of a magistrates’ court in England and Wales, to the
Crown Court;

1.303Z61.1.b

from an order or decision of the sheriff, to the Sheriff Appeal Court;

1.303Z61.1.c

from an order or decision of a magistrates’ court in Northern Ireland, to a
county court.

1.303Z61.2

An appeal under subsection  (1)  must be made before the end of the period of
30 days starting with the day on which the court makes the order or decision.

1.303Z61.3

The court hearing the appeal may make any order it thinks appropriate.

1.303Z61.4

If the court upholds an appeal against an order forfeiting the converted
cryptoassets, it may order the release of some or all of the converted
cryptoassets.

########### Application of forfeited converted cryptoassets

1.303Z62

1.303Z62.1

Converted cryptoassets detained under section  303Z57  and forfeited under
section  303Z60 , and any accrued interest on them, must be applied as
follows—

1.303Z62.1.a

first, they must be applied in making any payment of reasonable expenses
incurred by an enforcement officer in connection with the safe storage of the
cryptoassets mentioned in section  303Z57 (1)  during the period the
cryptoassets were detained under Chapter 3C;

1.303Z62.1.b

second, they must be applied in making any payment of reasonable expenses
incurred by an enforcement officer in connection with the conversion of those
cryptoassets under section  303Z54 (6) ;

1.303Z62.1.c

third, they must be applied in making any payment of reasonable expenses
incurred by an enforcement officer in connection with the detention of the
converted cryptoassets under this Chapter;

1.303Z62.1.d

fourth, they must be paid—

1.303Z62.1.d.i

if forfeited by a magistrates’ court in England and Wales or Northern Ireland,
into the Consolidated Fund, and

1.303Z62.1.d.ii

if forfeited by the sheriff, into the Scottish Consolidated Fund.

1.303Z62.2

Converted cryptoassets detained under section  303Z58  and forfeited under
section  303Z60 , and any accrued interest on them, must be applied as
follows—

1.303Z62.2.a

first, they must be applied in making any payment of reasonable expenses
incurred by an enforcement officer in connection with the detention of the
converted cryptoassets under this Chapter;

1.303Z62.2.b

second, they must be paid—

1.303Z62.2.b.i

if forfeited by a magistrates’ court in England and Wales or Northern Ireland,
into the Consolidated Fund, and

1.303Z62.2.b.ii

if forfeited by the sheriff, into the Scottish Consolidated Fund.

1.303Z62.3

But converted cryptoassets are not to be applied or paid under subsection  (1)
or  (2) —

1.303Z62.3.a

before the end of the period within which an appeal under section  303Z61  may
be made, or

1.303Z62.3.b

if a person appeals under that section, before the appeal is determined or
otherwise disposed of.

########## Supplementary

########### Victims and other owners

1.303Z63

1.303Z63.1

This section applies where converted cryptoassets are detained under this
Chapter.

1.303Z63.2

Where this section applies, a person (“ P ”) who claims that the relevant
cryptoassets belonged to P immediately before—

1.303Z63.2.a

the relevant cryptoassets were seized, or

1.303Z63.2.b

the crypto wallet freezing order was made in relation to the crypto wallet in
which the relevant cryptoassets were held,

may apply to the relevant court for some or all of the converted cryptoassets
to be released to P.

1.303Z63.3

The application may be made in the course of proceedings under section  303Z57
,  303Z58  or  303Z60  or at any other time.

1.303Z63.4

The relevant court may order the converted cryptoassets to which the
application relates to be released to the applicant if it appears to the
relevant court that the condition in subsection  (5)  is met.

1.303Z63.5

The condition in this subsection is that—

1.303Z63.5.a

the applicant was deprived of the relevant cryptoassets, or of property which
they represent, by unlawful conduct,

1.303Z63.5.b

the relevant cryptoassets the applicant was deprived of were not, immediately
before the applicant was deprived of them, recoverable property, and

1.303Z63.5.c

the relevant cryptoassets belonged to the applicant immediately before—

1.303Z63.5.c.i

the relevant cryptoassets were seized, or

1.303Z63.5.c.ii

the crypto wallet freezing order was made in relation to the crypto wallet in
which the relevant cryptoassets were held.

1.303Z63.6

If subsection  (7)  applies, the relevant court may order the converted
cryptoassets to which the application relates to be released to the applicant
or to the person from whom the relevant cryptoassets were seized.

1.303Z63.7

This subsection applies where—

1.303Z63.7.a

the applicant is not the person from whom the relevant cryptoassets were
seized,

1.303Z63.7.b

it appears to the relevant court that the relevant cryptoassets belonged to
the applicant immediately before—

1.303Z63.7.b.i

the relevant cryptoassets were seized, or

1.303Z63.7.b.ii

the crypto wallet freezing order was made in relation to the crypto wallet in
which the relevant cryptoassets were held,

1.303Z63.7.c

the relevant court is satisfied that the release condition is met in relation
to the converted cryptoassets, and

1.303Z63.7.d

no objection to the making of an order under subsection  (6)  has been made by
the person from whom the relevant cryptoassets were seized.

1.303Z63.8

The release condition is met—

1.303Z63.8.a

if the conditions in this Chapter for the detention of the converted
cryptoassets are no longer met, or

1.303Z63.8.b

in relation to converted cryptoassets which are subject to an application for
forfeiture under section  303Z60 , if the court or sheriff decides not to make
an order under that section in relation to the converted cryptoassets.

1.303Z63.9

Where subsection  (2)(b)  applies, references in this section to a person from
whom relevant cryptoassets were seized include a reference to a person by or
for whom the crypto wallet mentioned in that provision was administered
immediately before the crypto wallet freezing order was made in relation to
the crypto wallet.

1.303Z63.10

In this section “ the relevant cryptoassets ” means—

1.303Z63.10.a

in relation to converted cryptoassets detained under section  303Z57 , some or
all of the cryptoassets mentioned in subsection  (1)  of that section, and

1.303Z63.10.b

in relation to converted cryptoassets detained under section  303Z58 , some or
all of the cryptoassets mentioned in subsection  (1)  of that section.

########### Compensation

1.303Z64

1.303Z64.1

This section applies if no order is made under section  303Z60  in respect of
converted cryptoassets detained under this Chapter.

1.303Z64.2

Where this section applies, the following may make an application to the
relevant court for compensation—

1.303Z64.2.a

a person to whom the relevant cryptoassets belonged immediately before they
were seized;

1.303Z64.2.b

a person from whom the relevant cryptoassets were seized;

1.303Z64.2.c

a person by or for whom the crypto wallet mentioned in section  303Z58 (1)
was administered immediately before the crypto wallet freezing order was made
in relation to the crypto wallet.

1.303Z64.3

If the relevant court is satisfied that—

1.303Z64.3.a

the applicant has suffered loss as a result of—

1.303Z64.3.a.i

the conversion of the relevant cryptoassets into money, or

1.303Z64.3.a.ii

the detention of the converted cryptoassets, and

1.303Z64.3.b

the circumstances are exceptional,

the relevant court may order compensation to be paid to the applicant.

1.303Z64.4

The amount of compensation to be paid is the amount the relevant court thinks
reasonable, having regard to the loss suffered and any other relevant
circumstances.

1.303Z64.5

If the relevant cryptoassets were seized, or the relevant crypto wallet
freezing order was applied for, by an officer of Revenue and Customs, the
compensation is to be paid by the Commissioners for His Majesty’s Revenue and
Customs.

1.303Z64.6

If the relevant cryptoassets were seized, or the relevant crypto wallet
freezing order was applied for, by a constable, the compensation is to be paid
as follows—

1.303Z64.6.a

in the case of a constable of a police force in England and Wales, it is to be
paid out of the police fund from which the expenses of the police force are
met;

1.303Z64.6.b

in the case of a constable of the Police Service of Scotland, it is to be paid
by the Scottish Police Authority;

1.303Z64.6.c

in the case of a police officer within the meaning of the Police (Northern
Ireland) Act 2000, it is to be paid out of money provided by the Chief
Constable of the Police Service of Northern Ireland.

1.303Z64.7

If the relevant cryptoassets were seized, or the relevant crypto wallet
freezing order was applied for, by an SFO officer, the compensation is to be
paid by the Director of the Serious Fraud Office.

1.303Z64.8

If the relevant cryptoassets were seized, or the relevant crypto wallet
freezing order was applied for, by a National Crime Agency officer, the
compensation is to be paid by the National Crime Agency.

1.303Z64.9

If the relevant cryptoassets were seized, or the relevant crypto wallet
freezing order was applied for, by an accredited financial investigator who
was not an officer of Revenue and Customs, a constable, an SFO officer or a
National Crime Agency officer, the compensation is to be paid as follows—

1.303Z64.9.a

in the case of an investigator who was—

1.303Z64.9.a.i

a member of the civilian staff of a police force (including the metropolitan
police force), within the meaning of Part 1 of the Police Reform and Social
Responsibility Act 2011, or

1.303Z64.9.a.ii

a member of staff of the City of London police force,

it is to be paid out of the police fund from which the expenses of the police
force are met,

1.303Z64.9.b

in the case of an investigator who was a member of staff of the Police Service
of Northern Ireland, it is to be paid out of money provided by the Chief
Constable of the Police Service of Northern Ireland,

1.303Z64.9.c

in the case of an investigator who was a member of staff of a department of
the Government of the United Kingdom, it is to be paid by the Minister of the
Crown in charge of the department or by the department,

1.303Z64.9.d

in the case of an investigator who was a member of staff of a Northern Ireland
department, it is to be paid by the department,

1.303Z64.9.e

in the case of an investigator who was exercising a function of the Welsh
Revenue Authority, it is to be paid by the Welsh Revenue Authority, and

1.303Z64.9.f

in any other case, it is to be paid by the employer of the investigator.

1.303Z64.10

The Secretary of State may by regulations amend subsection  (9) .

1.303Z64.11

The power in subsection  (10)  is exercisable by the Department of Justice
(and not by the Secretary of State) so far as it may be used to make provision
that—

1.303Z64.11.a

would be within the legislative competence of the Northern Ireland Assembly if
contained in an Act of that Assembly, and

1.303Z64.11.b

would not, if contained in a Bill for an Act of the Northern Ireland Assembly,
result in the Bill requiring the consent of the Secretary of State.

1.303Z64.12

In this section—

“ the relevant cryptoassets ” means— in relation to converted cryptoassets
detained under section  303Z57 , the cryptoassets mentioned in subsection  (1)
of that section; in relation to converted cryptoassets detained under section
303Z58 , the cryptoassets mentioned in subsection  (1)  of that section; “ the
relevant crypto wallet freezing order ”, in relation to converted cryptoassets
detained under section  303Z58 , means the crypto wallet freezing order
mentioned in subsection  (1)  of that section.

########### Powers for prosecutors to appear in proceedings

1.303Z65

1.303Z65.1

The Director of Public Prosecutions or the Director of Public Prosecutions for
Northern Ireland may appear for a constable or an accredited financial
investigator in proceedings under this Chapter if the Director—

1.303Z65.1.a

is asked by, or on behalf of, a constable or (as the case may be) an
accredited financial investigator to do so, and

1.303Z65.1.b

considers it appropriate to do so.

1.303Z65.2

The Director of Public Prosecutions may appear for the Commissioners for His
Majesty’s Revenue and Customs or an officer of Revenue and Customs in
proceedings under this Chapter if the Director—

1.303Z65.2.a

is asked by, or on behalf of, the Commissioners for His Majesty’s Revenue and
Customs or (as the case may be) an officer of Revenue and Customs to do so,
and

1.303Z65.2.b

considers it appropriate to do so.

1.303Z65.3

The Directors may charge fees for the provision of services under this
section.

1.303Z65.4

The references in subsection  (1)  to an accredited financial investigator do
not include an accredited financial investigator who is an officer of Revenue
and Customs but the references in subsection  (2)  to an officer of Revenue
and Customs do include an accredited financial investigator who is an officer
of Revenue and Customs.

########## Interpretation

########### Interpretation

1.303Z66

1.303Z66.1

In this Chapter—

“ converted cryptoassets ” is to be read in accordance with sections  303Z57
and  303Z58 ; “ crypto wallet freezing order ” has the same meaning as in
Chapter 3D (see section  303Z36 ); “ enforcement officer ” has the meaning
given by section  303Z20 ; “ relevant court ” means— in England and Wales and
Northern Ireland, a magistrates’ court, and in Scotland, the sheriff; “
relevant financial institution ” has the meaning given by section 303Z1(6); “
UK-connected cryptoasset service provider ” has the meaning given by section
303Z36 .

1.303Z66.2

Section  303Z36 (4)(b)  applies in relation to this Chapter as it applies in
relation to Chapter 3D.

1.303Z66.3

In this Chapter references to the conversion of cryptoassets into money are
references to the conversion of cryptoassets into—

1.303Z66.3.a

cash, or

1.303Z66.3.b

money held in an account maintained with a relevant financial institution.

Before section 303Z18 (but after the italic heading “Supplementary”) insert—

############ Victims and other owners

6.5.303Z17A

6.5.303Z17A.1

A person who claims that money in respect of which an account freezing order
has effect belongs to them may apply for the money to be released.

6.5.303Z17A.2

An application under subsection  (1)  is to be made—

6.5.303Z17A.2.a

in England and Wales or Northern Ireland, to a magistrates’ court;

6.5.303Z17A.2.b

in Scotland, to the sheriff.

6.5.303Z17A.3

The application may be made in the course of proceedings under section 303Z3
or 303Z14 or at any other time.

6.5.303Z17A.4

The court or sheriff may, subject to subsection (8), order the money to which
the application relates to be released to the applicant if it appears to the
court or sheriff that—

6.5.303Z17A.4.a

the applicant was deprived of the money to which the application relates, or
of property which it represents, by unlawful conduct,

6.5.303Z17A.4.b

the money the applicant was deprived of was not, immediately before the
applicant was deprived of it, recoverable property, and

6.5.303Z17A.4.c

the money belongs to the applicant.

6.5.303Z17A.5

If subsection  (6)  applies, the court or sheriff may, subject to subsection
(8), order the money to which the application relates to be released to the
applicant.

6.5.303Z17A.6

This subsection applies where—

6.5.303Z17A.6.a

the applicant is not the person from whom the money to which the application
relates was seized,

6.5.303Z17A.6.b

it appears to the court or sheriff that the money belongs to the applicant,

6.5.303Z17A.6.c

the court or sheriff is satisfied that the release condition is met in
relation to the money, and

6.5.303Z17A.6.d

no objection to the making of an order under subsection  (5)  has been made by
the person from whom the money was seized.

6.5.303Z17A.7

The release condition is met—

6.5.303Z17A.7.a

in relation to money held in a frozen account, if the conditions for making an
order under section 303Z3 in relation to the money are no longer met, or

6.5.303Z17A.7.b

in relation to money held in a frozen account which is subject to an
application for forfeiture under section 303Z14, if the court or sheriff
decides not to make an order under that section in relation to the money.

6.5.303Z17A.8

Money is not to be released under this section—

6.5.303Z17A.8.a

if an account forfeiture notice under section 303Z9 is given in respect of the
money, until any proceedings in pursuance of the notice (including any
proceedings on appeal) are concluded;

6.5.303Z17A.8.b

if an application for its forfeiture under section 303Z14 is made, until any
proceedings in pursuance of the application (including any proceedings on
appeal) are concluded.

6.5.303Z17A.9

In relation to money held in an account that is subject to an account freezing
order, references in this section to a person from whom money was seized
include a reference to a person by or for whom the account was operated
immediately before the account freezing order was made.

After section 311 insert—

############ Chapters 3C to 3F: supplementary

############# Financial investigators

6.6.311A

detention of cryptoassets etc),

applies for forfeiture under section 303Z41 or 303Z60 (forfeiture of
cryptoassets etc), or

6.6.311A.1.c

brings an appeal under, or relating to, Chapter 3E or 3F (cryptoassets etc).

6.6.311A.2

Any subsequent step in the application or appeal, or any further application
or appeal relating to the same matter, may be taken, made or brought by a
different accredited financial investigator of the same description.

8.2

In section 341 (investigations), after subsection (3C) insert—

8.2.3D

For the purposes of this Part a cryptoasset investigation is an investigation
for the purposes of Chapter 3C, 3D, 3E or 3F of Part 5 and includes
investigation into—

8.2.3D.a

the derivation of cryptoassets detained under Chapter 3C (including where the
cryptoassets have been converted into money in accordance with Chapter 3F),

8.2.3D.b

whether cryptoassets or converted cryptoassets detained under Chapter 3C or 3F
are intended by any person to be used in unlawful conduct,

8.2.3D.c

the derivation of cryptoassets held in a crypto wallet in relation to which a
crypto wallet freezing order made under section  303Z37  has effect (including
where the cryptoassets have been converted into money in accordance with
Chapter 3F), or

8.2.3D.d

whether cryptoassets held in such a wallet are intended by any person to be
used in unlawful conduct.

8.3

after “frozen funds investigation” insert  “, a cryptoasset investigation” .

8.4

investigation” substitute  “, a frozen funds investigation or a cryptoasset
investigation” .

8.5

Cryptoassets: terrorism

Section 181

##### Amendments to the Anti-terrorism, Crime and Security Act 2001

1

Schedule 1 to the Anti-terrorism, Crime and Security Act 2001 (forfeiture of
terrorist property) is amended as follows.

2

After Part 4B insert—

######### Seizure and detention of terrorist cryptoassets

########## Interpretation

2.10Z7A

2.10Z7A.1

In this Schedule—

“ cryptoasset ” means a cryptographically secured digital representation of
value or contractual rights that uses a form of distributed ledger technology
and can be transferred, stored or traded electronically; “ crypto wallet ”
means— software, hardware, a physical item, or any combination of the things
mentioned in paragraphs  (a)  to  (c) , which is used to store the
cryptographic private key that allows cryptoassets to be accessed; “ terrorist
cryptoasset ” means a cryptoasset which— is within subsection (1)(a) or (b) of
section 1, or is earmarked as terrorist property.

2.10Z7A.2

The Secretary of State may by regulations made by statutory instrument amend
the definitions of “cryptoasset” and “crypto wallet” in sub-paragraph  (1) .

2.10Z7A.3

Regulations under sub-paragraph  (2) —

2.10Z7A.3.a

may make different provision for different purposes;

2.10Z7A.3.b

may make consequential, supplementary, incidental, transitional, transitory or
saving provision.

2.10Z7A.4

A statutory instrument containing regulations under sub-paragraph  (2)  may
not be made unless a draft of the instrument has been laid before and approved
by a resolution of each House of Parliament.

2.10Z7A.5

In this Part—

“ cryptoasset-related item ” means an item of property that is, or that
contains or gives access to information that is, likely to assist in the
seizure under this Part of terrorist cryptoassets; “ senior officer ” means— a
senior police officer; an officer of Revenue and Customs of a rank designated
by the Commissioners for His Majesty’s Revenue and Customs as equivalent to
that of a senior police officer; an immigration officer of a rank designated
by the Secretary of State as equivalent to that of a senior police officer; “
senior police officer ” means a police officer of at least the rank of
superintendent.

########## Seizure of cryptoasset-related items

2.10Z7AA

2.10Z7AA.1

An authorised officer may seize any item of property if the authorised officer
has reasonable grounds for suspecting that the item is a cryptoasset-related
item.

2.10Z7AA.2

If an authorised officer is lawfully on any premises, the officer may, for the
purpose of—

2.10Z7AA.2.a

determining whether any property is a cryptoasset-related item, or

2.10Z7AA.2.b

enabling or facilitating the seizure under this Part of any terrorist
cryptoasset,

require any information which is stored in any electronic form and accessible
from the premises to be produced in a form in which it can be taken away and
in which it is visible and legible, or from which it can readily be produced
in a visible and legible form.

2.10Z7AA.3

But sub-paragraph  (2)  does not authorise an authorised officer to require a
person to produce privileged information.

2.10Z7AA.4

In this paragraph “ privileged information ” means information which a person
would be entitled to refuse to provide—

2.10Z7AA.4.a

in England and Wales and Northern Ireland, on grounds of legal professional
privilege in proceedings in the High Court;

2.10Z7AA.4.b

in Scotland, on grounds of confidentiality of communications in proceedings in
the Court of Session.

2.10Z7AA.5

Where an authorised officer has seized a cryptoasset-related item under sub-
paragraph  (1) , the officer may use any information obtained from the item
for the purpose of—

2.10Z7AA.5.a

identifying or gaining access to a crypto wallet, and

2.10Z7AA.5.b

by doing so, enabling or facilitating the seizure under this Part of any
cryptoassets.

########## Initial detention of cryptoasset-related items

2.10Z7AB

2.10Z7AB.1

Property seized under paragraph  10Z7AA  may be detained for an initial period
of 48 hours.

2.10Z7AB.2

Sub-paragraph  (1)  authorises the detention of property only for so long as
an authorised officer continues to have reasonable grounds for suspicion in
relation to that property as described in paragraph  10Z7AA (1) .

2.10Z7AB.3

In calculating a period of 48 hours for the purposes of this paragraph, no
account is to be taken of—

2.10Z7AB.3.a

any Saturday or Sunday,

2.10Z7AB.3.b

Christmas Day,

2.10Z7AB.3.c

Good Friday,

2.10Z7AB.3.d

any day that is a bank holiday under the Banking and Financial Dealings Act
1971 in the part of the United Kingdom within which the property is seized, or

2.10Z7AB.3.e

any day prescribed by virtue of section 8(2) of the Criminal Procedure
(Scotland) Act 1995 as a court holiday in a sheriff court in the sheriff court
district within which the property is seized.

########## Further detention of cryptoasset-related items

2.10Z7AC

2.10Z7AC.1

The period for which property seized under paragraph  10Z7AA  may be detained
may be extended by an order made—

2.10Z7AC.1.a

in England and Wales or Northern Ireland, by a magistrates’ court;

2.10Z7AC.1.b

in Scotland, by the sheriff.

2.10Z7AC.2

An order under sub-paragraph  (1)  may not authorise the detention of any
property—

2.10Z7AC.2.a

beyond the end of the period of 6 months beginning with the date of the order,
and

2.10Z7AC.2.b

in the case of any further order under this paragraph, beyond the end of the
period of 2 years beginning with the date of the first order; but this is
subject to sub-paragraph  (4) .

2.10Z7AC.3

A justice of the peace may also exercise the power of a magistrates’ court to
make the first order under sub-paragraph  (1) .

2.10Z7AC.4

The court or sheriff may make an order for the period of 2 years in sub-
paragraph  (2)(b)  to be extended to a period of up to 3 years beginning with
the date of the first order.

2.10Z7AC.5

An application to a magistrates’ court, a justice of the peace or the sheriff
to make the first order under sub-paragraph  (1)  extending a particular
period of detention—

2.10Z7AC.5.a

may be made and heard without notice of the application or hearing having been
given to any of the persons affected by the application or to the legal
representatives of such a person, and

2.10Z7AC.5.b

may be heard and determined in private in the absence of persons so affected
and of their legal representatives.

2.10Z7AC.6

An application for an order under sub-paragraph  (1)  or  (4)  may be made—

2.10Z7AC.6.a

in relation to England and Wales and Northern Ireland, by the Commissioners
for His Majesty’s Revenue and Customs or an authorised officer;

2.10Z7AC.6.b

in relation to Scotland, by a procurator fiscal.

2.10Z7AC.7

The court, sheriff or justice may make an order under sub-paragraph  (1)  if
satisfied, in relation to the item of property to be further detained, that—

2.10Z7AC.7.a

there are reasonable grounds for suspecting that it is a cryptoasset-related
item, and

2.10Z7AC.7.b

its continuing detention is justified.

2.10Z7AC.8

The court or sheriff may make an order under sub-paragraph  (4)  if satisfied
that a request for assistance is outstanding in relation to the item of
property to be further detained.

2.10Z7AC.9

A “request for assistance” in sub-paragraph  (8)  means a request for
assistance in obtaining evidence (including information in any form or
article) in connection with the property to be further detained, made —

2.10Z7AC.9.a

by a judicial authority in the United Kingdom under section 7 of the Crime
(International Co-operation) Act 2003,

2.10Z7AC.9.b

by an authorised officer, to an authority exercising equivalent functions in a
foreign country,

2.10Z7AC.9.c

by the Scottish Ministers in connection with their functions under this
Schedule, to an authority exercising equivalent functions in a foreign
country, or

2.10Z7AC.9.d

by a person under section 375A or 408A of the Proceeds of Crime Act 2002
(evidence overseas).

2.10Z7AC.10

An order under sub-paragraph  (1)  must provide for notice to be given to
persons affected by the order.

########## Seizure of cryptoassets

2.10Z7AD

2.10Z7AD.1

An authorised officer may seize cryptoassets if the authorised officer has
reasonable grounds for suspecting that the cryptoassets are terrorist
cryptoassets.

2.10Z7AD.2

The circumstances in which a cryptoasset is “ seized ” for the purposes of
sub-paragraph  (1)  include circumstances in which it is transferred into a
crypto wallet controlled by the authorised officer.

########## Prior authorisation for detention of cryptoassets

2.10Z7AE

2.10Z7AE.1

Where an order is made under paragraph  10Z7AC  in respect of a cryptoasset-
related item, the court, sheriff or justice making the order may, at the same
time, make an order to authorise the detention of any cryptoassets that may be
seized as a result of information obtained from that item.

2.10Z7AE.2

An application for an order under this paragraph may be made, by a person
mentioned in paragraph  10Z7AC (6) , at the same time as an application for an
order under paragraph  10Z7AC  is made by that person.

2.10Z7AE.3

The court, sheriff or justice may make an order under this paragraph if
satisfied that there are reasonable grounds for suspecting that the
cryptoassets that may be seized are terrorist cryptoassets.

2.10Z7AE.4

An order under this paragraph authorises detention of the cryptoassets for the
same period of time as the order under paragraph  10Z7AC  authorises detention
in respect of the cryptoasset-related item to which those cryptoassets relate.

########## Initial detention of cryptoassets

2.10Z7AF

2.10Z7AF.1

Cryptoassets seized under paragraph  10Z7AD  may be detained for an initial
period of 48 hours.

2.10Z7AF.2

Sub-paragraph  (1)  authorises the detention of cryptoassets only for so long
as an authorised officer continues to have reasonable grounds for suspicion in
relation to those cryptoassets as described in paragraph  10Z7AD (1) .

2.10Z7AF.3

In calculating a period of 48 hours for the purposes of this paragraph, no
account is to be taken of—

2.10Z7AF.3.a

any Saturday or Sunday,

2.10Z7AF.3.b

Christmas Day,

2.10Z7AF.3.c

Good Friday,

2.10Z7AF.3.d

any day that is a bank holiday under the Banking and Financial Dealings Act
1971 in the part of the United Kingdom within which the property is seized, or

2.10Z7AF.3.e

any day prescribed by virtue of section 8(2) of the Criminal Procedure
(Scotland) Act 1995 as a court holiday in a sheriff court in the sheriff court
district within which the property is seized.

2.10Z7AF.4

This paragraph is subject to paragraph  10Z7AE .

########## Further detention of cryptoassets

2.10Z7AG

2.10Z7AG.1

The period for which cryptoassets seized under paragraph  10Z7AD  may be
detained may be extended by an order made—

2.10Z7AG.1.a

in England and Wales or Northern Ireland, by a magistrates’ court;

2.10Z7AG.1.b

in Scotland, by the sheriff.

2.10Z7AG.2

An order under sub-paragraph  (1)  may not authorise the detention of any
cryptoassets—

2.10Z7AG.2.a

beyond the end of the period of 6 months beginning with the date of the order,
and

2.10Z7AG.2.b

in the case of any further order under this paragraph, beyond the end of the
period of 2 years beginning with the date of the first order; but this is
subject to sub-paragraph  (4) .

2.10Z7AG.3

A justice of the peace may also exercise the power of a magistrates’ court to
make the first order under sub-paragraph  (1) .

2.10Z7AG.4

The court or sheriff may make an order for the period of 2 years in sub-
paragraph  (2)(b)  to be extended to a period of up to 3 years beginning with
the date of the first order.

2.10Z7AG.5

An application to a magistrates’ court, a justice of the peace or the sheriff
to make the first order under sub-paragraph  (1)  extending a particular
period of detention—

2.10Z7AG.5.a

may be made and heard without notice of the application or hearing having been
given to any of the persons affected by the application or to the legal
representatives of such a person, and

2.10Z7AG.5.b

may be heard and determined in private in the absence of persons so affected
and of their legal representatives.

2.10Z7AG.6

An application for an order under sub-paragraph  (1)  or  (4)  may be made—

2.10Z7AG.6.a

in relation to England and Wales and Northern Ireland, by the Commissioners
for His Majesty’s Revenue and Customs or an authorised officer;

2.10Z7AG.6.b

in relation to Scotland, by a procurator fiscal.

2.10Z7AG.7

The court, sheriff or justice may make an order under sub-paragraph  (1)  if
satisfied, in relation to the cryptoassets to be further detained, that
condition 1, condition 2 or condition 3 is met.

2.10Z7AG.8

Condition 1 is that there are reasonable grounds for suspecting that the
cryptoassets are intended to be used for the purposes of terrorism and that
either—

2.10Z7AG.8.a

their continued detention is justified while their intended use is further
investigated or consideration is given to bringing (in the United Kingdom or
elsewhere) proceedings against any person for an offence with which the
cryptoassets are connected, or

2.10Z7AG.8.b

proceedings against any person for an offence with which the cryptoassets are
connected have been started and have not been concluded.

2.10Z7AG.9

Condition 2 is that there are reasonable grounds for suspecting that the
cryptoassets consist of resources of an organisation which is a proscribed
organisation and that either—

2.10Z7AG.9.a

their continued detention is justified while investigation is made into
whether or not they consist of such resources or consideration is given to
bringing (in the United Kingdom or elsewhere) proceedings against any person
for an offence with which the cryptoassets are connected, or

2.10Z7AG.9.b

proceedings against any person for an offence with which the cryptoassets are
connected have been started and have not been concluded.

2.10Z7AG.10

Condition 3 is that there are reasonable grounds for suspecting that the
cryptoassets are property earmarked as terrorist property and that either—

2.10Z7AG.10.a

their continued detention is justified while their derivation is further
investigated or consideration is given to bringing (in the United Kingdom or
elsewhere) proceedings against any person for an offence with which the
cryptoassets are connected, or

2.10Z7AG.10.b

proceedings against any person for an offence with which the cryptoassets are
connected have been started and have not been concluded.

2.10Z7AG.11

The court or sheriff may make an order under sub-paragraph  (4)  if satisfied
that a request for assistance is outstanding in relation to the cryptoassets
to be further detained.

2.10Z7AG.12

A “request for assistance” in sub-paragraph  (11)  means a request for
assistance in obtaining evidence (including information in any form or
article) in connection with the property to be further detained, made —

2.10Z7AG.12.a

by a judicial authority in the United Kingdom under section 7 of the Crime
(International Co-operation) Act 2003,

2.10Z7AG.12.b

by an authorised officer, to an authority exercising equivalent functions in a
foreign country,

2.10Z7AG.12.c

by the Scottish Ministers in connection with their functions under this
Schedule, to an authority exercising equivalent functions in a foreign
country, or

2.10Z7AG.12.d

by a person under section 375A or 408A of the Proceeds of Crime Act 2002
(evidence overseas).

2.10Z7AG.13

An order under sub-paragraph  (1)  must provide for notice to be given to
persons affected by the order.

########## Safekeeping of cryptoasset-related items and cryptoassets

2.10Z7AH

2.10Z7AH.1

An authorised officer must arrange for any item of property seized under
paragraph  10Z7AA  to be safely stored throughout the period during which it
is detained under this Part.

2.10Z7AH.2

An authorised officer must arrange for any cryptoassets seized under paragraph
10Z7AD  to be safely stored throughout the period during which they are
detained under this Part.

########## Release of cryptoasset-related items and cryptoassets

2.10Z7AI

2.10Z7AI.1

This paragraph applies while any cryptoasset or other item of property is
detained under this Part.

2.10Z7AI.2

A magistrates’ court or (in Scotland) the sheriff may, subject to sub-
paragraph  (9) , direct the release of the whole or any part of the property
if the following condition is met.

2.10Z7AI.3

The condition is that the court or sheriff is satisfied, on an application by
the person from whom the property was seized, that the conditions for the
detention of the property in this Part are no longer met in relation to the
property to be released.

2.10Z7AI.4

A person within sub-paragraph  (5)  may, subject to sub-paragraph  (9)  and
after notifying the magistrates’ court, sheriff or justice under whose order
property is being detained, release the whole or any part of the property if
satisfied that the detention of the property to be released is no longer
justified.

2.10Z7AI.5

The following persons are within this sub-paragraph—

2.10Z7AI.5.a

in relation to England and Wales and Northern Ireland, an authorised officer;

2.10Z7AI.5.b

in relation to Scotland, a procurator fiscal.

2.10Z7AI.6

If any cryptoasset-related item which has been released is not claimed within
the period of a year beginning with the date on which it was released, an
authorised officer may—

2.10Z7AI.6.a

retain the item and deal with it as they see fit,

2.10Z7AI.6.b

dispose of the item, or

2.10Z7AI.6.c

destroy the item.

2.10Z7AI.7

The powers in sub-paragraph  (6)  may be exercised only—

2.10Z7AI.7.a

where the authorised officer has taken reasonable steps to notify—

2.10Z7AI.7.a.i

the person from whom the item was seized, and

2.10Z7AI.7.a.ii
